</th>

</td></tr>

</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Slavonic Dances
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Slovanské tance
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Dvo%C5%99%C3%A1k,_Anton%C3%ADn" title="Category:Dvořák, Antonín">Dvořák, Antonín</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.46&#160;; B.78 (piano duet), B.83 (orchestration)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IAD 81
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 dances:
<ol><li> <i>Furiant</i>. Presto (C major)
</li><li> <i>Dumka</i>. Allegretto scherzando–Allegro vivo (E minor)
</li><li> <i>Polka</i>. Poco Allegro (A<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> major)
</li><li> <i>Sousedská</i>. Tempo di menuetto (F major)
</li><li> <i>Skocná</i>. Allegro vivace (A major)
</li><li> <i>Sousedská</i>. Allegretto scherzando (D major)
</li><li> <i>Skocná</i>. Allegro assai (C minor)
</li><li> <i>Furiant</i>. Presto (G minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1878 (piano duet, orchestra)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1878-05-16 in Prague (<i>Orchestration</i>, Nos.1, 3, 4)<br />1878-12-04 and 18 in Dresden (<i>Orchestration</i>, Nos.1–4, 5–8)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1878 (piano duet, orchestra)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>38 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>piano 4-hands, orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd>piccolo, 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons<br />4 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones<br />timpani, bass drum, cymbals, triangle, strings </div>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
